  description: Maps each level to an evenly spaced hue on the colour wheel and then convert them with ggplotly.

# Default plot


<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))

plotly::ggplotly(d)
</pre>

# Change colour hue



<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue()

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

`clarity` is the default hue.


<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue("clarity")

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

You can also use expression functions.



<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(expression(clarity[beta]))

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

# Adjust luminocity and chroma



<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(l = 40, c = 30)

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(l = 70, c = 30)

plotly::ggplotly(p)

<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(l = 70, c = 150)

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(l = 80, c = 150)

dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(h = c(0, 90))

plotly::ggplotly(p)

# Adjust range of hues used



<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(h = c(0, 90))

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(h = c(90, 180))

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(h = c(180, 270))

plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

<pre class="mcode">
dsamp <- diamonds[sample(nrow(diamonds), 1000), ]
d <- ggplot(dsamp, aes(carat, price)) + geom_point(aes(colour = clarity))
p <-  d + scale_colour_hue(h = c(270, 360))

plotly::ggplotly(p)

# Colour missing values


<pre class="mcode">
miss <- factor(sample(c(NA, 1:5), nrow(mtcars), replace = TRUE))
p <-    
 ggplot(mtcars, aes(mpg, wt)) +
  geom_point(aes(colour = miss))
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

<pre class="mcode">
miss <- factor(sample(c(NA, 1:5), nrow(mtcars), replace = TRUE))
p <-    
 ggplot(mtcars, aes(mpg, wt)) +
  geom_point(aes(colour = miss)) +
  scale_colour_hue(na.value = "black")
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>
